## 数据开发-

### 周期任务-

#### 基本操作

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 在对应目录新建文件夹成功 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，“目录名称”输入“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，“目录名称”输入“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 文件夹新建失败，提示：文件夹已存在 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，文件夹成功移至对应目录，且文件夹名称与修改后的一致 |  |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，“目录名称”修改为“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，“目录名称”修改为“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 文件夹编辑失败，提示：同一路径下不能存在同名文件夹 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹（文件夹为空），右键“删除”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹（文件夹为空），右键“删除”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 对应文件夹删除成功 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹（文件夹不为空），右键“删除”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹（文件夹不为空），右键“删除”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 对应文件夹删除失败，提示：目录非空 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，点击“新建任务”，“周期任务名称”填写不存在的名称，正确填写其余内容，点击“确定”

| 2 | 2）在对应的目录下新增对应的周期任务 |  |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】页面，选择一条周期任务记录，右键“编辑”，“周期任务名称”修改为不存在的名称，正确修改其余内容，点击“确定”

#### 数据同步

##### 【P2】验证数据同步任务正常_mysql2mysql_成功_主键冲突为insert into

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |

##### 【P2】进入【数据开发-周期任务】，新建周期任务，“周期任务类型”选择“数据同步”，“配置模式”选择“向导模式”，“同步模式”选择“无增量标识”，填写其余内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【数据开发-周期任务】，新建周期任务，“周期任务类型”选择“数据同步”，“配置模式”选择“向导模式”，“同步模式”选择“无增量标识”，填写其余内容，点击“确定” | 数据同步任务新建成功 |

##### 【P2】【数据来源】步骤，选择mysql数据源，“配置方式”选择“选择库表”，其余内容正常填写

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，1）点击“数据预览”：正确展示3条数据 |  |
| 2 | 2）点击“下一步”：进入【选择目标】步骤 |  |

##### 【P2】【选择目标】步骤，选择mysql数据源，“主键冲突”选择“insert into（当主键/约束冲突，报脏数据）”，“导入前准备语句”输入“INSERT INTO mysql_demo_data_types_source (tiny_int_col, small_int_col) VALUES (66,77);”，其余内容正常填写

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，1）点击“一键生成目标表”：进入【建表语句】弹窗，展示对应的建表语句 | 2）点击“建表语句”的“确定”：建表成功 |
| 2 |  | 3）再次一键生成目标表，表名为已存在，点击“确定”：建表失败 |
| 3 | 4）点击“下一步”：进入【字段映射】步骤 |  |

##### 【P2】【数据来源】步骤，选择mysql数据源，“配置方式”选择“自定义SQL”，其余内容正常填写，自定义sql如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，select id ,tiny_int_col ,small_int_col ,medium_int_col,big_int_col from mysql_demo_data_types_source where id>=1; |  |
| 2 | 1）点击“数据预览”：正确展示3条数据 |  |
| 3 | 2）点击“下一步”：进入【选择目标】步骤 |  |

##### 【P2】【选择目标】步骤，选择mysql数据源，“主键冲突”选择“replace into（当主键/约束冲突，先delete再insert，未映射的字段会被映射为NULL）”，“导入后准备语句”输入“delete from mysql_demo_data_types_source where id =1;”，其余内容正常填写


> 用例步骤

| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，drop table if exists mysql_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mysql_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 整数类型 |  |
| 4 | id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID', |  |
| 5 | tiny_int_col TINYINT COMMENT '小整数(-128~127)', |  |
| 6 | small_int_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整数(-32768~32767)', |  |
| 7 | medium_int_col MEDIUMINT COMMENT '中等整数', |  |
| 8 | big_int_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整数', |  |
| 9 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 10 | float_col FLOAT(8,2) COMMENT '单精度浮点数', |  |
| 11 | double_col DOUBLE(16,4) COMMENT '双精度浮点数', |  |
| 12 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 13 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 14 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '定长字符串', |  |
| 15 | varchar_col VARCHAR(255) COMMENT '变长字符串', |  |
| 16 | text_col TEXT COMMENT '长文本', |  |
| 17 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 18 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期', |  |
| 19 | time_col TIME COMMENT '时间', |  |
| 20 | datetime_col DATETIME COMMENT '日期时间', |  |
| 21 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳', |  |
| 22 | year_col YEAR COMMENT '年份', |  |
| 23 | -- 枚举和集合类型 |  |
| 24 | enum_col ENUM('1', '2', '3') COMMENT '枚举类型', |  |
| 25 | set_col SET('1', '2', '3', '4') COMMENT '集合类型', |  |
| 26 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 27 | bool_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔值', |  |
| 28 | -- JSON类型 (MySQL 5.7+) |  |
| 29 | json_col JSON COMMENT 'JSON数据' |  |
| 30 | ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='常用数据类型示例表'; | mysql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

| 14 | daai.api_id = daa.id |  |

| 16 | dap.id = daa.project_id |  |
| 17 | left join mysql_test_da_tenant dat on |  |
| 18 | dat.id = daa.tenant_id |  |
| 19 | group by |  |
| 20 | daai.api_id ) t |  |
| 21 | order by |  |

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- 创建使用HASH分布模型的表 |  |
| 2 | drop table if exists doris_demo_data_types; |  |
| 3 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS doris_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 4 | -- Hash分布列（常用于查询和分布的列） |  |
| 5 | user_id BIGINT COMMENT "用户ID", |  |
| 6 | created_date DATE COMMENT "创建日期", |  |
| 7 | -- 其他业务字段 |  |
| 8 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT "姓名", |  |
| 9 | age TINYINT COMMENT "年龄", |  |
| 10 | status SMALLINT COMMENT "状态码", |  |
| 11 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 12 | price DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT "价格", |  |
| 13 | weight FLOAT COMMENT "重量", |  |
| 14 | rating DOUBLE COMMENT "评分", |  |
| 15 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 16 | description STRING COMMENT "描述信息", |  |
| 17 | gender VARCHAR(10) COMMENT "性别", |  |
| 18 | department VARCHAR(20) COMMENT "部门", |  |
| 19 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 20 | created_time DATETIME COMMENT "创建时间", |  |
| 21 | birth_date DATE COMMENT "出生日期", |  |
| 22 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 23 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT "是否激活", |  |
| 24 | -- 其他类型 |  |
| 25 | tags VARCHAR(100) COMMENT "标签", |  |
| 26 | -- 数值型字段 |  |
| 27 | total_amount BIGINT COMMENT "总金额", |  |
| 28 | order_count INT COMMENT "订单数量" |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | ENGINE=olap |  |
| 31 | DUPLICATE KEY(user_id, created_date, name)  -- 查询常用的列作为Duplicate Key |  |
| 32 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(user_id) BUCKETS 10  -- 使用user_id作为Hash分布列 |  |
| 33 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 34 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 35 | ); | doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- 基础查询 |  |
| 2 | SELECT name, age, salary |  |
| 3 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 4 | WHERE is_active = TRUE |  |
| 5 | ORDER BY salary DESC LIMIT 10; |  |
| 6 | -- 分组查询 |  |
| 7 | SELECT region, SUM(amount) AS total_sales |  |
| 8 | FROM doris_sales_records |  |
| 9 | WHERE sale_date BETWEEN '2023-01-01' AND '2023-12-31' |  |
| 10 | GROUP BY region; |  |
| 11 | -- 子查询 |  |
| 12 | SELECT name, salary |  |
| 13 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 14 | WHERE salary > (SELECT AVG(salary) FROM doris_user_profile); |  |
| 15 | -- join操作 |  |
| 16 | SELECT u.name, s.amount, s.sale_date |  |
| 17 | FROM doris_user_profile u JOIN doris_sales_records s ON u.id = s.user_id |  |
| 18 | WHERE s.region = 'East'; | 1）doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 19 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，drop table if exists starrocks_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS starrocks_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 主键列必须放在前面 |  |
| 4 | id BIGINT COMMENT '用户ID，主键', |  |
| 5 | partition_date DATE COMMENT '分区字段', |  |
| 6 | -- 其他数值类型 |  |
| 7 | age TINYINT(6) COMMENT '年龄', |  |
| 8 | score DOUBLE COMMENT '评分', |  |
| 9 | salary DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT '薪水', |  |
| 10 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 11 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '姓名', |  |
| 12 | description STRING COMMENT '描述', |  |
| 13 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 14 | create_date DATE COMMENT '创建日期', |  |
| 15 | create_time DATETIME COMMENT '创建时间', |  |
| 16 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 17 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT '是否活跃', |  |
| 18 | -- 数组类型 |  |
| 19 | tags ARRAY<VARCHAR(20)> COMMENT '标签数组', |  |
| 20 | -- JSON类型 |  |
| 21 | extra_info JSON COMMENT '额外信息' |  |
| 22 | ) |  |
| 23 | ENGINE = OLAP |  |
| 24 | PRIMARY KEY (id, partition_date)  -- 主键列顺序与表结构中的顺序一致 |  |
| 25 | PARTITION BY RANGE (partition_date) ( |  |
| 26 | PARTITION p202401 VALUES [('2024-01-01'), ('2024-02-01')), |  |
| 27 | PARTITION p202402 VALUES [('2024-02-01'), ('2024-03-01')), |  |
| 28 | PARTITION p202403 VALUES [('2024-03-01'), ('2024-04-01')) |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(id) BUCKETS 8 |  |
| 31 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 32 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 33 | ); | starrocks sql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

##### 【P2】输入sql脚本，点击“运行”，sql脚本如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- DQL 1: 条件过滤 |  |
| 2 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE total_price > 500; |  |
| 3 | -- DQL 2: 分组聚合 |  |
| 4 | SELECT product_id, SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity FROM starrocks_orders GROUP BY product_id; | -- DQL 3: 排序分页 |
| 5 | SELECT customer_id, SUM(total_price) AS total_amount |  |
| 6 | FROM starrocks_orders |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY customer_id |  |
| 8 | ORDER BY total_amount DESC |  |
| 9 | LIMIT 5; |  |
| 10 | -- DQL 4: 子查询 |  |
| 11 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE product_id IN (SELECT product_id FROM starrocks_products WHERE category = 'Electronics'); |  |
| 12 | -- DQL 5: CASE WHEN |  |
| 13 | SELECT product_name, |  |
| 14 | CASE WHEN price < 500 THEN 'Low' |  |
| 15 | WHEN price BETWEEN 500 AND 1000 THEN 'Medium' |  |
| 16 | ELSE 'High' |  |
| 17 | END AS price_level |  |
| 18 | FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 19 | -- DQL 6: DISTINCT 去重 |  |
| 20 | SELECT DISTINCT category FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 21 | -- DQL 7: JOIN 连接 |  |
| 22 | SELECT o.order_id, c.name AS customer_name, o.total_price |  |
| 23 | FROM starrocks_orders o JOIN starrocks_customers c ON o.customer_id = c.customer_id; |  |
| 24 | -- DQL 8: LEFT JOIN + NULL 判断 |  |
| 25 | SELECT c.name AS customer_name |  |
| 26 | FROM starrocks_customers c LEFT JOIN starrocks_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id |  |
| 27 | WHERE o.order_id IS NULL; | 1）starrocks sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 28 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 60 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳类型', |  |

| 65 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 66 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 67 | )stored as textfile ; |  |
| 68 | -- parquet表 |  |


> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）hive sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 67 | )stored as textfile ; |  |
| 68 | -- parquet表 |  |

| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 49 | small_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整型', |  |
| 50 | big_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整型', |  |
| 51 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 52 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |
| 53 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 54 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 55 | string_col STRING COMMENT '字符串类型', |  |
| 56 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 57 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 58 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 59 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期类型', |  |
| 60 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳类型', |  |
| 61 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 62 | boolean_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔类型', |  |
| 63 | -- 复杂类型 |  |
| 64 | array_col ARRAY<STRING> COMMENT '数组类型', |  |
| 65 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 66 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 67 | )stored as parquet; | spark sql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |


| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【周期任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

### 手动任务-

#### 基本操作

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 在对应目录新建文件夹成功 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，“目录名称”输入“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，点击“新建文件夹”，“目录名称”输入“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 文件夹新建失败，提示：文件夹已存在 |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，文件夹成功移至对应目录，且文件夹名称与修改后的一致 |  |

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，“目录名称”修改为“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-手动任务】页面，选择非根节点的文件夹，右键“编辑”，“目录名称”修改为“同一级已存在的目录名称”，正确填写所有内容，点击“确定” | 文件夹编辑失败，提示：同一路径下不能存在同名文件夹 |

| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mysql_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 整数类型 |  |
| 4 | id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID', |  |
| 5 | tiny_int_col TINYINT COMMENT '小整数(-128~127)', |  |
| 6 | small_int_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整数(-32768~32767)', |  |
| 7 | medium_int_col MEDIUMINT COMMENT '中等整数', |  |
| 8 | big_int_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整数', |  |
| 9 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 10 | float_col FLOAT(8,2) COMMENT '单精度浮点数', |  |
| 11 | double_col DOUBLE(16,4) COMMENT '双精度浮点数', |  |
| 12 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 13 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 14 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '定长字符串', |  |
| 15 | varchar_col VARCHAR(255) COMMENT '变长字符串', |  |
| 16 | text_col TEXT COMMENT '长文本', |  |
| 17 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 18 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期', |  |
| 19 | time_col TIME COMMENT '时间', |  |
| 20 | datetime_col DATETIME COMMENT '日期时间', |  |
| 21 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳', |  |
| 22 | year_col YEAR COMMENT '年份', |  |
| 23 | -- 枚举和集合类型 |  |
| 24 | enum_col ENUM('1', '2', '3') COMMENT '枚举类型', |  |
| 25 | set_col SET('1', '2', '3', '4') COMMENT '集合类型', |  |
| 26 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 27 | bool_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔值', |  |
| 28 | -- JSON类型 (MySQL 5.7+) |  |
| 29 | json_col JSON COMMENT 'JSON数据' |  |
| 30 | ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='常用数据类型示例表'; | mysql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，select * from mysql_test_1 where 1 = 1 and id > 0  and name like 'demo' and last_name in ('a'); |  |
| 2 | select * from mysql_test_2_a  union all select * from mysql_test_2_b union all select * from mysql_test_2_c; |  |
| 3 | select |  |
| 4 | t.api_id, |  |
| 5 | t.cnt |  |
| 6 | from |  |
| 7 | ( |  |
| 8 | select |  |
| 9 | daai.api_id, |  |
| 10 | COUNT(*) as cnt |  |
| 11 | from |  |
| 12 | mysql_test_apply_invoke daai |  |
| 13 | left join mysql_test_da_api daa on |  |
| 14 | daai.api_id = daa.id |  |
| 15 | left join mysql_test_da_project dap on |  |
| 16 | dap.id = daa.project_id |  |
| 17 | left join mysql_test_da_tenant dat on |  |
| 18 | dat.id = daa.tenant_id |  |
| 19 | group by |  |
| 20 | daai.api_id ) t |  |
| 21 | order by |  |
| 22 | t.cnt; | 1）mysql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 23 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 创建使用HASH分布模型的表 |  |
| 2 | drop table if exists doris_demo_data_types; |  |
| 3 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS doris_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 4 | -- Hash分布列（常用于查询和分布的列） |  |
| 5 | user_id BIGINT COMMENT "用户ID", |  |
| 6 | created_date DATE COMMENT "创建日期", |  |
| 7 | -- 其他业务字段 |  |
| 8 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT "姓名", |  |
| 9 | age TINYINT COMMENT "年龄", |  |
| 10 | status SMALLINT COMMENT "状态码", |  |
| 11 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 12 | price DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT "价格", |  |
| 13 | weight FLOAT COMMENT "重量", |  |
| 14 | rating DOUBLE COMMENT "评分", |  |
| 15 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 16 | description STRING COMMENT "描述信息", |  |
| 17 | gender VARCHAR(10) COMMENT "性别", |  |
| 18 | department VARCHAR(20) COMMENT "部门", |  |
| 19 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 20 | created_time DATETIME COMMENT "创建时间", |  |
| 21 | birth_date DATE COMMENT "出生日期", |  |
| 22 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 23 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT "是否激活", |  |
| 24 | -- 其他类型 |  |
| 25 | tags VARCHAR(100) COMMENT "标签", |  |
| 26 | -- 数值型字段 |  |
| 27 | total_amount BIGINT COMMENT "总金额", |  |
| 28 | order_count INT COMMENT "订单数量" |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | ENGINE=olap |  |
| 31 | DUPLICATE KEY(user_id, created_date, name)  -- 查询常用的列作为Duplicate Key |  |
| 32 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(user_id) BUCKETS 10  -- 使用user_id作为Hash分布列 |  |
| 33 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 34 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 35 | ); | doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 基础查询 |  |
| 2 | SELECT name, age, salary |  |
| 3 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 4 | WHERE is_active = TRUE |  |
| 5 | ORDER BY salary DESC LIMIT 10; |  |
| 6 | -- 分组查询 |  |
| 7 | SELECT region, SUM(amount) AS total_sales |  |
| 8 | FROM doris_sales_records |  |
| 9 | WHERE sale_date BETWEEN '2023-01-01' AND '2023-12-31' |  |
| 10 | GROUP BY region; |  |
| 11 | -- 子查询 |  |
| 12 | SELECT name, salary |  |
| 13 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 14 | WHERE salary > (SELECT AVG(salary) FROM doris_user_profile); |  |
| 15 | -- join操作 |  |
| 16 | SELECT u.name, s.amount, s.sale_date |  |
| 17 | FROM doris_user_profile u JOIN doris_sales_records s ON u.id = s.user_id |  |
| 18 | WHERE s.region = 'East'; | 1）doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 19 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，drop table if exists starrocks_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS starrocks_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 主键列必须放在前面 |  |
| 4 | id BIGINT COMMENT '用户ID，主键', |  |
| 5 | partition_date DATE COMMENT '分区字段', |  |
| 6 | -- 其他数值类型 |  |
| 7 | age TINYINT(6) COMMENT '年龄', |  |
| 8 | score DOUBLE COMMENT '评分', |  |
| 9 | salary DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT '薪水', |  |
| 10 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 11 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '姓名', |  |
| 12 | description STRING COMMENT '描述', |  |
| 13 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 14 | create_date DATE COMMENT '创建日期', |  |
| 15 | create_time DATETIME COMMENT '创建时间', |  |
| 16 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 17 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT '是否活跃', |  |
| 18 | -- 数组类型 |  |
| 19 | tags ARRAY<VARCHAR(20)> COMMENT '标签数组', |  |
| 20 | -- JSON类型 |  |
| 21 | extra_info JSON COMMENT '额外信息' |  |
| 22 | ) |  |
| 23 | ENGINE = OLAP |  |
| 24 | PRIMARY KEY (id, partition_date)  -- 主键列顺序与表结构中的顺序一致 |  |
| 25 | PARTITION BY RANGE (partition_date) ( |  |
| 26 | PARTITION p202401 VALUES [('2024-01-01'), ('2024-02-01')), |  |
| 27 | PARTITION p202402 VALUES [('2024-02-01'), ('2024-03-01')), |  |
| 28 | PARTITION p202403 VALUES [('2024-03-01'), ('2024-04-01')) |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(id) BUCKETS 8 |  |
| 31 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 32 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 33 | ); | starrocks sql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

##### 【P2】输入sql脚本，点击“运行”，sql脚本如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- DQL 1: 条件过滤 |  |
| 2 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE total_price > 500; |  |
| 3 | -- DQL 2: 分组聚合 |  |
| 4 | SELECT product_id, SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity FROM starrocks_orders GROUP BY product_id; | -- DQL 3: 排序分页 |
| 5 | SELECT customer_id, SUM(total_price) AS total_amount |  |
| 6 | FROM starrocks_orders |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY customer_id |  |
| 8 | ORDER BY total_amount DESC |  |
| 9 | LIMIT 5; |  |
| 10 | -- DQL 4: 子查询 |  |
| 11 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE product_id IN (SELECT product_id FROM starrocks_products WHERE category = 'Electronics'); |  |
| 12 | -- DQL 5: CASE WHEN |  |
| 13 | SELECT product_name, |  |
| 14 | CASE WHEN price < 500 THEN 'Low' |  |
| 15 | WHEN price BETWEEN 500 AND 1000 THEN 'Medium' |  |
| 16 | ELSE 'High' |  |
| 17 | END AS price_level |  |
| 18 | FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 19 | -- DQL 6: DISTINCT 去重 |  |
| 20 | SELECT DISTINCT category FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 21 | -- DQL 7: JOIN 连接 |  |
| 22 | SELECT o.order_id, c.name AS customer_name, o.total_price |  |
| 23 | FROM starrocks_orders o JOIN starrocks_customers c ON o.customer_id = c.customer_id; |  |
| 24 | -- DQL 8: LEFT JOIN + NULL 判断 |  |
| 25 | SELECT c.name AS customer_name |  |
| 26 | FROM starrocks_customers c LEFT JOIN starrocks_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id |  |
| 27 | WHERE o.order_id IS NULL; | 1）starrocks sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 28 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）hive sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 基本类型数据表 |  |
| 2 | drop table if exists spark_temp_basic_data; |  |
| 3 | CREATE TABLE if not exists spark_temp_basic_data ( |  |
| 4 | id INT, |  |
| 5 | tiny_col TINYINT, |  |
| 6 | small_col SMALLINT, |  |
| 7 | big_col BIGINT, |  |
| 8 | float_col FLOAT, |  |
| 9 | double_col DOUBLE, |  |
| 10 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2), |  |
| 11 | string_col STRING, |  |
| 12 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50), |  |
| 13 | char_col CHAR(10), |  |
| 14 | date_col DATE, |  |
| 15 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP, |  |
| 16 | boolean_col BOOLEAN |  |
| 17 | )stored as orc; |  |
| 18 | -- orc表 |  |
| 19 | drop table if exists spark_orc_demo_data_types; |  |
| 20 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_orc_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 21 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 22 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |
| 23 | tiny_col TINYINT COMMENT '微小整型', |  |
| 24 | small_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整型', |  |
| 25 | big_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整型', |  |
| 26 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 27 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |
| 28 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 29 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 30 | string_col STRING COMMENT '字符串类型', |  |
| 31 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 32 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 33 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 34 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期类型', |  |
| 35 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳类型', |  |
| 36 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 37 | boolean_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔类型', |  |
| 38 | -- 复杂类型 |  |
| 39 | array_col ARRAY<STRING> COMMENT '数组类型', |  |
| 40 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 41 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 42 | )stored as orc; |  |
| 43 | --textfile表 |  |
| 44 | drop table if exists spark_textfile_demo_data_types; |  |
| 45 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_textfile_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 46 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 47 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |
| 48 | tiny_col TINYINT COMMENT '微小整型', |  |
| 49 | small_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整型', |  |
| 50 | big_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整型', |  |
| 51 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 52 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |
| 53 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 54 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 55 | string_col STRING COMMENT '字符串类型', |  |
| 56 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 57 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 58 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 59 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期类型', |  |
| 60 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳类型', |  |
| 61 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 62 | boolean_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔类型', |  |
| 63 | -- 复杂类型 |  |
| 64 | array_col ARRAY<STRING> COMMENT '数组类型', |  |
| 65 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 66 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 67 | )stored as textfile ; |  |
| 68 | -- parquet表 |  |
| 69 | drop table if exists spark_parquet_demo_data_types; |  |
| 70 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_parquet_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 71 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 72 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |
| 73 | tiny_col TINYINT COMMENT '微小整型', |  |
| 74 | small_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整型', |  |
| 75 | big_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整型', |  |
| 76 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 77 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |

| 81 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 82 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 83 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 84 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期类型', |  |

##### 【P2】输入sql脚本，点击“运行”，sql脚本如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 26 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 27 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |

| 29 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 30 | string_col STRING COMMENT '字符串类型', |  |
| 31 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 32 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 33 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |

| 38 | -- 复杂类型 |  |

| 40 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 41 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 42 | )stored as orc; |  |
| 43 | -- parquet表 |  |
| 44 | drop table if exists spark_parquet_demo_data_types; |  |
| 45 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_parquet_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 46 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 47 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |
| 48 | tiny_col TINYINT COMMENT '微小整型', |  |

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【手动任务-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mysql_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 整数类型 |  |
| 4 | id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID', |  |
| 5 | tiny_int_col TINYINT COMMENT '小整数(-128~127)', |  |
| 6 | small_int_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整数(-32768~32767)', |  |
| 7 | medium_int_col MEDIUMINT COMMENT '中等整数', |  |
| 8 | big_int_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整数', |  |
| 9 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 10 | float_col FLOAT(8,2) COMMENT '单精度浮点数', |  |
| 11 | double_col DOUBLE(16,4) COMMENT '双精度浮点数', |  |
| 12 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 13 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 14 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '定长字符串', |  |
| 15 | varchar_col VARCHAR(255) COMMENT '变长字符串', |  |
| 16 | text_col TEXT COMMENT '长文本', |  |
| 17 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 18 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期', |  |
| 19 | time_col TIME COMMENT '时间', |  |
| 20 | datetime_col DATETIME COMMENT '日期时间', |  |
| 21 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳', |  |
| 22 | year_col YEAR COMMENT '年份', |  |
| 23 | -- 枚举和集合类型 |  |
| 24 | enum_col ENUM('1', '2', '3') COMMENT '枚举类型', |  |
| 25 | set_col SET('1', '2', '3', '4') COMMENT '集合类型', |  |
| 26 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 27 | bool_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔值', |  |
| 28 | -- JSON类型 (MySQL 5.7+) |  |
| 29 | json_col JSON COMMENT 'JSON数据' |  |
| 30 | ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='常用数据类型示例表'; | mysql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

| 5 | t.cnt |  |
| 6 | from |  |
| 7 | ( |  |
| 8 | select |  |
| 9 | daai.api_id, |  |

| 11 | from |  |

| 16 | dap.id = daa.project_id |  |
| 17 | left join mysql_test_da_tenant dat on |  |
| 18 | dat.id = daa.tenant_id |  |
| 19 | group by |  |
| 20 | daai.api_id ) t |  |
| 21 | order by |  |
| 22 | t.cnt; | 1）mysql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 创建使用HASH分布模型的表 |  |
| 2 | drop table if exists doris_demo_data_types; |  |
| 3 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS doris_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 4 | -- Hash分布列（常用于查询和分布的列） |  |
| 5 | user_id BIGINT COMMENT "用户ID", |  |
| 6 | created_date DATE COMMENT "创建日期", |  |
| 7 | -- 其他业务字段 |  |
| 8 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT "姓名", |  |
| 9 | age TINYINT COMMENT "年龄", |  |
| 10 | status SMALLINT COMMENT "状态码", |  |
| 11 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 12 | price DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT "价格", |  |
| 13 | weight FLOAT COMMENT "重量", |  |
| 14 | rating DOUBLE COMMENT "评分", |  |
| 15 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 16 | description STRING COMMENT "描述信息", |  |
| 17 | gender VARCHAR(10) COMMENT "性别", |  |
| 18 | department VARCHAR(20) COMMENT "部门", |  |
| 19 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 20 | created_time DATETIME COMMENT "创建时间", |  |
| 21 | birth_date DATE COMMENT "出生日期", |  |
| 22 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 23 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT "是否激活", |  |
| 24 | -- 其他类型 |  |
| 25 | tags VARCHAR(100) COMMENT "标签", |  |
| 26 | -- 数值型字段 |  |
| 27 | total_amount BIGINT COMMENT "总金额", |  |
| 28 | order_count INT COMMENT "订单数量" |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | ENGINE=olap |  |
| 31 | DUPLICATE KEY(user_id, created_date, name)  -- 查询常用的列作为Duplicate Key |  |
| 32 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(user_id) BUCKETS 10  -- 使用user_id作为Hash分布列 |  |
| 33 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 34 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 35 | ); | doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 基础查询 |  |
| 2 | SELECT name, age, salary |  |
| 3 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 4 | WHERE is_active = TRUE |  |
| 5 | ORDER BY salary DESC LIMIT 10; |  |
| 6 | -- 分组查询 |  |
| 7 | SELECT region, SUM(amount) AS total_sales |  |
| 8 | FROM doris_sales_records |  |
| 9 | WHERE sale_date BETWEEN '2023-01-01' AND '2023-12-31' |  |
| 10 | GROUP BY region; |  |
| 11 | -- 子查询 |  |
| 12 | SELECT name, salary |  |
| 13 | FROM doris_user_profile |  |
| 14 | WHERE salary > (SELECT AVG(salary) FROM doris_user_profile); |  |
| 15 | -- join操作 |  |
| 16 | SELECT u.name, s.amount, s.sale_date |  |
| 17 | FROM doris_user_profile u JOIN doris_sales_records s ON u.id = s.user_id |  |
| 18 | WHERE s.region = 'East'; | 1）doris sql任务在对应的集群运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 19 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |


> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，drop table if exists starrocks_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS starrocks_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 主键列必须放在前面 |  |
| 4 | id BIGINT COMMENT '用户ID，主键', |  |
| 5 | partition_date DATE COMMENT '分区字段', |  |
| 6 | -- 其他数值类型 |  |
| 7 | age TINYINT(6) COMMENT '年龄', |  |
| 8 | score DOUBLE COMMENT '评分', |  |
| 9 | salary DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT '薪水', |  |
| 10 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 11 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '姓名', |  |
| 12 | description STRING COMMENT '描述', |  |
| 13 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 14 | create_date DATE COMMENT '创建日期', |  |
| 15 | create_time DATETIME COMMENT '创建时间', |  |
| 16 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 17 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT '是否活跃', |  |
| 18 | -- 数组类型 |  |
| 19 | tags ARRAY<VARCHAR(20)> COMMENT '标签数组', |  |
| 20 | -- JSON类型 |  |
| 21 | extra_info JSON COMMENT '额外信息' |  |
| 22 | ) |  |
| 23 | ENGINE = OLAP |  |
| 24 | PRIMARY KEY (id, partition_date)  -- 主键列顺序与表结构中的顺序一致 |  |
| 25 | PARTITION BY RANGE (partition_date) ( |  |
| 26 | PARTITION p202401 VALUES [('2024-01-01'), ('2024-02-01')), |  |
| 27 | PARTITION p202402 VALUES [('2024-02-01'), ('2024-03-01')), |  |
| 28 | PARTITION p202403 VALUES [('2024-03-01'), ('2024-04-01')) |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(id) BUCKETS 8 |  |
| 31 | PROPERTIES ( |  |
| 32 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 33 | ); | starrocks sql任务运行成功，数据表在底层创建成功 |

| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，select 1; | starrocks sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |

##### 【P2】输入sql脚本，点击“运行”，sql脚本如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- DQL 1: 条件过滤 |  |
| 2 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE total_price > 500; |  |
| 3 | -- DQL 2: 分组聚合 |  |
| 4 | SELECT product_id, SUM(quantity) AS total_quantity FROM starrocks_orders GROUP BY product_id; | -- DQL 3: 排序分页 |
| 5 | SELECT customer_id, SUM(total_price) AS total_amount |  |
| 6 | FROM starrocks_orders |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY customer_id |  |
| 8 | ORDER BY total_amount DESC |  |
| 9 | LIMIT 5; |  |
| 10 | -- DQL 4: 子查询 |  |
| 11 | SELECT * FROM starrocks_orders WHERE product_id IN (SELECT product_id FROM starrocks_products WHERE category = 'Electronics'); |  |
| 12 | -- DQL 5: CASE WHEN |  |
| 13 | SELECT product_name, |  |
| 14 | CASE WHEN price < 500 THEN 'Low' |  |
| 15 | WHEN price BETWEEN 500 AND 1000 THEN 'Medium' |  |
| 16 | ELSE 'High' |  |
| 17 | END AS price_level |  |
| 18 | FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 19 | -- DQL 6: DISTINCT 去重 |  |
| 20 | SELECT DISTINCT category FROM starrocks_products; |  |
| 21 | -- DQL 7: JOIN 连接 |  |
| 22 | SELECT o.order_id, c.name AS customer_name, o.total_price |  |
| 23 | FROM starrocks_orders o JOIN starrocks_customers c ON o.customer_id = c.customer_id; |  |
| 24 | -- DQL 8: LEFT JOIN + NULL 判断 |  |
| 25 | SELECT c.name AS customer_name |  |
| 26 | FROM starrocks_customers c LEFT JOIN starrocks_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id |  |
| 27 | WHERE o.order_id IS NULL; | 1）starrocks sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 28 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 7 | big_col BIGINT, |  |

| 40 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |

##### 【P2】输入sql脚本，点击“运行”，sql脚本如下：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM hive_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）hive sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 基本类型数据表 |  |
| 2 | drop table if exists spark_temp_basic_data; |  |
| 3 | CREATE TABLE if not exists spark_temp_basic_data ( |  |
| 4 | id INT, |  |
| 5 | tiny_col TINYINT, |  |
| 6 | small_col SMALLINT, |  |
| 7 | big_col BIGINT, |  |
| 8 | float_col FLOAT, |  |
| 9 | double_col DOUBLE, |  |
| 10 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2), |  |
| 11 | string_col STRING, |  |
| 12 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50), |  |
| 13 | char_col CHAR(10), |  |
| 14 | date_col DATE, |  |
| 15 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP, |  |
| 16 | boolean_col BOOLEAN |  |
| 17 | )stored as orc; |  |
| 18 | -- orc表 |  |
| 19 | drop table if exists spark_orc_demo_data_types; |  |
| 20 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_orc_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 21 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 22 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |
| 23 | tiny_col TINYINT COMMENT '微小整型', |  |
| 24 | small_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整型', |  |
| 25 | big_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整型', |  |
| 26 | float_col FLOAT COMMENT '单精度浮点', |  |
| 27 | double_col DOUBLE COMMENT '双精度浮点', |  |
| 28 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 29 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 30 | string_col STRING COMMENT '字符串类型', |  |
| 31 | varchar_col VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '可变长度字符串', |  |
| 32 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '固定长度字符串', |  |
| 33 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 34 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期类型', |  |
| 35 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳类型', |  |
| 36 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 37 | boolean_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔类型', |  |
| 38 | -- 复杂类型 |  |
| 39 | array_col ARRAY<STRING> COMMENT '数组类型', |  |
| 40 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 41 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 42 | )stored as orc; |  |
| 43 | --textfile表 |  |
| 44 | drop table if exists spark_textfile_demo_data_types; |  |
| 45 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS spark_textfile_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 46 | -- 数值类型 |  |
| 47 | id INT COMMENT '整型ID', |  |

| 61 | -- 布尔类型 |  |

| 63 | -- 复杂类型 |  |
| 64 | array_col ARRAY<STRING> COMMENT '数组类型', |  |
| 65 | map_col MAP<STRING, INT> COMMENT '映射类型', |  |
| 66 | struct_col STRUCT<name:STRING, age:INT> COMMENT '结构体类型' |  |
| 67 | )stored as textfile ; |  |
| 68 | -- parquet表 |  |

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

| 5 | tiny_col TINYINT, |  |
| 6 | small_col SMALLINT, |  |
| 7 | big_col BIGINT, |  |
| 8 | float_col FLOAT, |  |

| 10 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2), |  |

| 15 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP, |  |

| 17 | )stored as orc; |  |

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【临时查询-】页面，-- 聚合函数 |  |
| 2 | SELECT id, |  |
| 3 | MIN(tiny_col) AS min_tiny_col, |  |
| 4 | MAX(tiny_col) AS max_tiny_col, |  |
| 5 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col |  |
| 6 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 7 | GROUP BY id; |  |
| 8 | SELECT |  |
| 9 | id, |  |
| 10 | AVG(tiny_col) AS avg_tiny_col, |  |
| 11 | COUNT(*) AS review_count, |  |
| 12 | SUM(small_col) AS total_small_col |  |
| 13 | FROM spark_orc_demo_data_types |  |
| 14 | GROUP BY id |  |
| 15 | HAVING avg_tiny_col >= 1; | 1）spark sql任务运行成功，展示结果正确 |
| 16 | 2）【结果】点击“下载”：下载结果与sql查询结果一致 |  |

### 表查询

#### 验证表查询功能正常_mysql

##### 【P2】超管账号登录，进入【离线开发-数据开发-周期任务】，新增mysql任务，输入sql后，临时运行，sql脚本：

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【表查询】页面，drop table if exists mysql_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mysql_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 整数类型 |  |
| 4 | id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID', |  |
| 5 | tiny_int_col TINYINT COMMENT '小整数(-128~127)', |  |
| 6 | small_int_col SMALLINT COMMENT '小整数(-32768~32767)', |  |
| 7 | medium_int_col MEDIUMINT COMMENT '中等整数', |  |
| 8 | big_int_col BIGINT COMMENT '大整数', |  |
| 9 | -- 浮点数类型 |  |
| 10 | float_col FLOAT(8,2) COMMENT '单精度浮点数', |  |
| 11 | double_col DOUBLE(16,4) COMMENT '双精度浮点数', |  |
| 12 | decimal_col DECIMAL(10,2) COMMENT '精确小数', |  |
| 13 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 14 | char_col CHAR(10) COMMENT '定长字符串', |  |
| 15 | varchar_col VARCHAR(255) COMMENT '变长字符串', |  |
| 16 | text_col TEXT COMMENT '长文本', |  |
| 17 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 18 | date_col DATE COMMENT '日期', |  |
| 19 | time_col TIME COMMENT '时间', |  |
| 20 | datetime_col DATETIME COMMENT '日期时间', |  |
| 21 | timestamp_col TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '时间戳', |  |

| 25 | set_col SET('1', '2', '3', '4') COMMENT '集合类型', |  |
| 26 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 27 | bool_col BOOLEAN COMMENT '布尔值', |  |
| 28 | -- JSON类型 (MySQL 5.7+) |  |
| 29 | json_col JSON COMMENT 'JSON数据' |  |
| 30 | ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='常用数据类型示例表'; |  |


> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【表查询】页面，drop table if exists starrocks_demo_data_types; |  |
| 2 | CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS starrocks_demo_data_types ( |  |
| 3 | -- 主键列必须放在前面 |  |
| 4 | id BIGINT COMMENT '用户ID，主键', |  |
| 5 | partition_date DATE COMMENT '分区字段', |  |
| 6 | -- 其他数值类型 |  |
| 7 | age TINYINT(6) COMMENT '年龄', |  |
| 8 | score DOUBLE COMMENT '评分', |  |
| 9 | salary DECIMAL(10, 2) COMMENT '薪水', |  |
| 10 | -- 字符串类型 |  |
| 11 | name VARCHAR(50) COMMENT '姓名', |  |
| 12 | description STRING COMMENT '描述', |  |
| 13 | -- 日期时间类型 |  |
| 14 | create_date DATE COMMENT '创建日期', |  |
| 15 | create_time DATETIME COMMENT '创建时间', |  |
| 16 | -- 布尔类型 |  |
| 17 | is_active BOOLEAN COMMENT '是否活跃', |  |
| 18 | -- 数组类型 |  |
| 19 | tags ARRAY<VARCHAR(20)> COMMENT '标签数组', |  |
| 20 | -- JSON类型 |  |
| 21 | extra_info JSON COMMENT '额外信息' |  |
| 22 | ) |  |
| 23 | ENGINE = OLAP |  |
| 24 | PRIMARY KEY (id, partition_date)  -- 主键列顺序与表结构中的顺序一致 |  |
| 25 | PARTITION BY RANGE (partition_date) ( |  |
| 26 | PARTITION p202401 VALUES [('2024-01-01'), ('2024-02-01')), |  |
| 27 | PARTITION p202402 VALUES [('2024-02-01'), ('2024-03-01')), |  |
| 28 | PARTITION p202403 VALUES [('2024-03-01'), ('2024-04-01')) |  |
| 29 | ) |  |
| 30 | DISTRIBUTED BY HASH(id) BUCKETS 8 |  |

| 32 | "replication_num" = "1" |  |
| 33 | ); |  |

#### 发布至本项目

##### 【P2】进入【离线开发-数据开发-任务发布-发布至本项目】页面，“发布包名称”输入“A”，“发布日期”选择“时间段BC”

> 前置条件
```
```

> 用例步骤

| 编号 | 步骤 | 预期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 进入【离线开发-数据开发-任务发布-发布至本项目】页面，“发布包名称”输入“A”，“发布日期”选择“时间段BC” | 列表展示：“发布包名称”包含“A”且“发布日期在时间段BC的所有已导入的发布包记录 |

##### 【P2】“发布人”选择“A”，“发布日期”选择“时间段BC”
